</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of <i>Top Gear</i> episodes</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div role="note" class="hatnote">This article is about the episodes from the 2002 television series. For the original format episodes, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_Top_Gear_(original_format)_episodes" title="List of Top Gear (original format) episodes">List of Top Gear (original format) episodes</a>. For the American television series, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_Top_Gear_(U.S.)_episodes" title="List of Top Gear (U.S.) episodes">List of Top Gear (U.S.) episodes</a>. For the Australian television series, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_Top_Gear_Australia_episodes" title="List of Top Gear Australia episodes">List of Top Gear Australia episodes</a>.</div>
<div class="floatright"><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_(2002_TV_series)" title="Top Gear (2002 TV series)"><img alt="TopGearLogo.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/TopGearLogo.svg/250px-TopGearLogo.svg.png" width="250" height="78" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/TopGearLogo.svg/375px-TopGearLogo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/TopGearLogo.svg/500px-TopGearLogo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="390" data-file-height="121" /></a></div>
<p>This <b>list of <i>Top Gear</i> episodes</b> consists of episodes from the 2002 format of the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> television series <i><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_(2002_TV_series)" title="Top Gear (2002 TV series)">Top Gear</a></i>, conceived by <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Clarkson" title="Jeremy Clarkson">Jeremy Clarkson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andy_Wilman" title="Andy Wilman">Andy Wilman</a>. For its first 22 series the programme was presented by Clarkson, <a href="/wiki/Richard_Hammond" title="Richard Hammond">Richard Hammond</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_May" title="James May">James May</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Stig" title="The Stig">The Stig</a>. Secondhand car specialist <a href="/wiki/Jason_Dawe_(TV_presenter)" class="mw-redirect" title="Jason Dawe (TV presenter)">Jason Dawe</a> was a co-presenter for the first series, but was replaced by May for the second series. In addition, there have been two shorter episodes produced for charity: <i><a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_of_the_Pops" title="Top Gear of the Pops">Top Gear of the Pops</a></i>, produced for Red Nose Day, and <i><a href="/wiki/Top_Ground_Gear_Force" title="Top Ground Gear Force">Top Ground Gear Force</a></i>, produced for <a href="/wiki/Sport_Relief" title="Sport Relief">Sport Relief</a>. These two episodes are not part of the episode count. There was also an <i><a href="/wiki/Ashes_to_Ashes_(TV_series)" title="Ashes to Ashes (TV series)">Ashes to Ashes</a></i> parody for BBC <a href="/wiki/Children_in_Need" title="Children in Need">Children in Need</a> which is not included.</p>
<p>A twenty-third series was commissioned and began airing on 29 May 2016. It is the first series following the departure of <a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Clarkson" title="Jeremy Clarkson">Clarkson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Richard_Hammond" title="Richard Hammond">Hammond</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_May" title="James May">May</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Chris_Evans_(presenter)" title="Chris Evans (presenter)">Chris Evans</a> as host.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Stig" title="The Stig">The Stig</a> still features in the new series.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>Episodes are listed in order of their original UK air date along with featured cars, challenges, and guests. For more information on features and challenges included in each series, visit each series' respective page. Comprehensive lists of challenges and races can be found at <a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_challenges" title="Top Gear challenges">Top Gear challenges</a> and <a href="/wiki/Top_Gear_Races" title="Top Gear Races">Top Gear Races</a>.</p>
<p>As of 3 July 2016<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Top_Gear_episodes&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, 184 episodes of the series, along with multiple special episodes, have been broadcast, spanning 23 series.</p>
<div style="clear: right; margin-bottom: .5em; float: right; padding: .5em 0 .8em 1.4em; background: none; width: auto;">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_episodes_.282015.29">Special episodes (2015)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Top_Gear_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Special episodes (2015)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In November 2015, the BBC announced "Top Gear: From A-Z", described as a "two-part extravaganza" in the form of a <a href="/wiki/Clip_show" title="Clip show">clip show</a> composed of material from the previous twenty-two series of <i>Top Gear</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[10]</a></sup> It is narrated by comedian <a href="/wiki/John_Bishop_(comedian)" title="John Bishop (comedian)">John Bishop</a> with celebrities presenting their favourite highlights from the show;<sup id="cite_ref-2106special_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2106special-52">[11]</a></sup> the programme did not use the <i>Top Gear</i> studio.<sup id="cite_ref-2106special_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2106special-52">[11]</a></sup></p>
